    "body": "## QA\r\nTo test, open a category page, and make sure that the Women's Bella Flowy Tank fits the card. \r\n\r\nNo Women's Bella Flowy campaign on a category page? Change the first cards image using this command in the console:\r\n`$('.card__image_container:first img').attr('src','http://vangogh.teespring.com/shirt_pic/2251629/2393281/95/2270/front.jpg?v=2015-04-28-03-19')` \r\n\r\n**IMPORTANT NOTE**: This fix was called out directly to address the Women's Bella Flowy Tank. Please note that this fix doesn't only affect those products, but other product types as well. During testing, please be on the lookout for any products that may also have cropping issues. Thanks!\r\n\r\n## Before:\r\n![screen shot 2015-05-04 at 3 04 11 pm](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/957232/7463507/e06c729e-f26e-11e4-8319-428d25724a7f.png)\r\n\r\n## After:\r\n#### Large media:\r\n![screen shot 2015-05-04 at 2 59 48 pm](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/957232/7463516/e957ca98-f26e-11e4-9fb4-82a442196349.png)\r\n\r\n#### Medium media:\r\n![screen shot 2015-05-04 at 2 59 56 pm](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/957232/7463521/ee6327ee-f26e-11e4-94a6-e9e256c89fc1.png)\r\n\r\n#### Small media:\r\n![screen shot 2015-05-04 at 3 00 11 pm](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/957232/7463533/f9b4d534-f26e-11e4-97f0-d655f408b00a.png)\r\n\r\n#### XSmall media\r\n![screen shot 2015-05-04 at 3 00 49 pm](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/957232/7463538/ff10fe18-f26e-11e4-9e87-fac665229f6f.png)\r\n",

    "body": "### Problem\r\n\r\nOur campaign page has gotten really slow. Like 1 second to render slow. 250ms of that is in the DB and there a lot of N+1 looking queries in there.\r\n\r\n### Solution\r\n\r\nUsed a shared campaign's products cache to get rid of the N+1 queries around products + colors. Also introduce a fragment cache around the campaign's info.\r\n\r\n###  QA Instructions\r\n\r\n1. Smoke test campaign page + different locales\r\n1. The size dimensions should stay the same\r\n1. Translations of the dimensions should show up properly\r\n1. The campaign info section should be correct\r\n1. The order of products + colors should stay the same",

    },
    "body": "The problem\r\n---------\r\nWhen tracking a visitor, a new session was created on every custom domain page and on every teespring.com campaign page instead of persisting the existing one.\r\n\r\nBecause Analytics was using POST to set the tracking session cookie, rails considered the request potentially harmful and therefore enforced the CSRF policy. \r\n\r\nThus on the campaign page, Analytics is unaware of the CSRF token and sends the request as usual, but a tracking cookie is never set. \r\n\r\nThis was also the case for custom domains. And it's especially more problematic due to the cross origin request limitation.\r\n\r\nThe solution \r\n---------\r\nJSONP request to enable cross-domain requests. And disabling CSRF verification for the cookie creation endpoint.",

      "events_url": "https://api.github.com/users/ekosz/events{/privacy}",
      "received_events_url": "https://api.github.com/users/ekosz/received_events",
      "type": "User",
      "site_admin": false
    },
    "body": "### Problem\r\n\r\nWe are losing money on sales of apparel for sizes 2XL and above. The reason being; the blank of those shirts are more expensive for us to buy, but we charge the buyer the same amount as a XS. Also we can't just naively charge more for those orders or that profit will just be paid out to the seller.\r\n\r\n### Solution\r\n\r\nBuild in the ability to charge more for certain prices while subtracting the difference for the seller's profit. The seller will continue to make the same amount of money per sale per product, but we get to recoup some of our losses.\r\n\r\nThe amount we increase the price by is equal to: `selling_price_of_product + (base_price_of_this_size - the_minimum_base_of_this_product_color_combo)`\r\n\r\nSo if the base price of a 2XL Red Hanes is $6.00 and the lowest base price of ALL Red Hanes is $4.00 and the campaign is selling Red Hanes for $24.00, we will sell the 2XL Red Hanes for $26.00.\r\n\r\nWhen the order is completed we will created a profit adjustment of: `selling_price_of_product_color - selling_price_of_line_item` or in the above example `$24.00 - $26.00` or `-$2.00`.\r\n\r\n### QA Instructions\r\n\r\n1. Work will Eric to set the base price of certain sizes\r\n1. On the campaign page, when those sizes are selected in the pre checkout model, the price should updated accordingly.\r\n1. When checking out, the price should reflect the increase\r\n1. After checking out, the order summary email should reflect the increase\r\n1. On the admin page for that order the prices should should reflect the increase\r\n1. When the campaign ends, those increases should not affect the seller's profit\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n1. Upsells should continue to work normally\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n1. Promo codes should continue to work normally  \r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n1. Make sure prices are reflected in reserving on an ended campaign as well",
